              <style>
  /*
    This is kind of gross but let me explain.
    The triangle-down icon in the user lists menu component needs to be larger on small screens
    but Primer doesn't accept a responsive value for size.
    So instead we use CSS to override the size on small screens only, to match the ⭐ button beside it.
    The selector is written this way to avoid affecting other buttons inside the lists dropdown.
  */
  @media (max-width: 767px) {
    .icon-button-group .BtnGroup-parent > * > button:first-child {
      height: var(--control-medium-size);
      width: var(--control-medium-size);
      min-width: var(--control-medium-size);
    }
  }

  /* No idea what this is though. It was like this when I got here. */
  @media (min-width: 544px) {
    .icon-button-group .SelectMenu {
      right: auto !important;
      left: 0 !important;
    }
  }
</style>

container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">MedGuide AI: Prescription Analyzer</h1><a id="user-content-medguide-ai-prescription-analyzer" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: MedGuide AI: Prescription Analyzer" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#medguide-ai-prescription-analyzer"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" <p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.python.org/downloads/" rel="nofollow"><img src="./REAMME_files/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f707974686f6e2d332e382b2d626c75652e737667" alt="Python 3.8+" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/python-3.8+-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://gradio.app/" rel="nofollow"><img src="./REAMME_files/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f67726164696f2d352e302b2d677265656e2e737667" alt="Gradio" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/gradio-5.0+-green.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://opensource.org/license/apache-2-0" rel="nofollow"><img src="./REAMME_files/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f4c6963656e73652d4170616368655f322e302d79656c6c6f772e737667" alt="License: Apache 2.0" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/License-Apache_2.0-yellow.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">A powerful AI-driven medical prescription analyzer that extracts medicine information from prescription images and provides comprehensive reports including prices, availability, dosage, and purchase links. Features a modern, clean interface with real-time streaming progress and collapsible sections for optimal user experience.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">✨ Key Features</h2><a id="user-content--key-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ✨ Key Features" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#-key-features"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔍 <strong>Advanced AI Analysis</strong></h3><a id="user-content--advanced-ai-analysis" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔍 Advanced AI Analysis" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#-advanced-ai-analysis"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Smart OCR</strong>: Extract medicine names from prescription images using Grok-4 AI</li>
<li><strong>Concurrent Processing</strong>: Fetch multiple medicine details simultaneously for faster results</li>
<li><strong>Real-time Streaming</strong>: Watch AI work step-by-step with live progress updates</li>
<li><strong>Optimized Performance</strong>: Ultra-fast medicine lookup with aggressive optimization and fallback handling</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎨 <strong>Modern User Interface</strong></h3><a id="user-content--modern-user-interface" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎨 Modern User Interface" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#-modern-user-interface"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Clean Design</strong>: Professional Gradio web interface with intuitive layout</li>
<li><strong>Smart Button States</strong>: Button automatically disables during processing to prevent duplicate requests</li>
<li><strong>Collapsible Logs</strong>: Optional detailed processing logs hidden by default for clean UX</li>
<li><strong>Collapsible Disclaimer</strong>: Important medical warnings in expandable section</li>
<li><strong>Responsive Layout</strong>: Optimized for both desktop and mobile viewing</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📋 <strong>Comprehensive Reports</strong></h3><a id="user-content--comprehensive-reports" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📋 Comprehensive Reports" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#-comprehensive-reports"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Live Report Streaming</strong>: Watch AI generate your medical report in real-time with streaming text updates</li>
<li><strong>Structured Information</strong>: Detailed markdown reports with medicine descriptions</li>
<li><strong>Price &amp; Availability</strong>: Real-time pricing and purchase information</li>
<li><strong>Processing Transparency</strong>: Full visibility into AI decision-making process</li>
<li><strong>Error Handling</strong>: Robust error handling with informative feedback</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🛠️ Technology Stack</h2><a id="user-content-️-technology-stack" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🛠️ Technology Stack" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#%EF%B8%8F-technology-stack"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>AI Model</strong>: Grok-4 by xAI for image analysis and text extraction</li>
<li><strong>Web Framework</strong>: Gradio for the user interface</li>
<li><strong>Data Source</strong>: Firecrawl API for medicine information retrieval</li>
<li><strong>Image Processing</strong>: PIL (Python Imaging Library)</li>
<li><strong>Concurrency</strong>: ThreadPoolExecutor for parallel processing</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📋 Prerequisites</h2><a id="user-content--prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📋 Prerequisites" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#-prerequisites"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Python 3.8 or higher</li>
<li>xAI API key (for Grok-4 access)</li>
<li>Firecrawl API key (for medicine data retrieval)</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎯 How to Use</h2><a id="user-content--how-to-use" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎯 How to Use" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#-how-to-use"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Basic Workflow</h3><a id="user-content-basic-workflow" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Basic Workflow" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#basic-workflow"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Upload Image</strong>: Click on the "Upload Prescription Image" area and select your prescription photo</li>
<li><strong>Analyze</strong>: Click the "Analyze Prescription" button (button automatically changes to "⏳ Processing..." and disables to prevent duplicate requests)</li>
<li><strong>Monitor Progress</strong>: Watch real-time processing updates in the main area and detailed logs in the collapsible section</li>
<li><strong>Live Streaming</strong>: Experience real-time report generation as the AI streams the final medical report text</li>
<li><strong>View Results</strong>: Get comprehensive medicine information including:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Medicine description and usage</li>
<li>Typical treatment duration</li>
<li>Price information and availability</li>
<li>Purchase links and sources</li>
<li>Total processing time</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🗂️ Interface Features</h3><a id="user-content-️-interface-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🗂️ Interface Features" href="https://github.com/kingabzpro/Medical-AI-with-Grok4#%EF%B8%8F-interface-features"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
